 kishor ke kisi bhi dal ke saath kaam karne kii pehali shart yah hoti he ki ve us netaa ke ghar se hi apane daftar kaa sanchaalan karte hai

 a large group joined the think tank India Foundation of Shaurya Doval, son of BJP General Secretary Ram Madhav and National Security Advisor Ajit Doval

 gane kii shooting kaa kuch hissaa in hastiyon par bhi filmaaya janaa tha

 baad main netaaon ke is dance kaa video viral ho gaya

 in There is no doubt that Amitabh Bachchan is the biggest magnate in the film industry
 is industry main unhone 5 dashakon kaa safar tay kar liya he
 During this, he gave a performance above one
 kariyar kii shuruyaat main sangharsh karne ke baad unhen zanjeer film se safalataa mili or ve industry main engri yang main ke naam se mashhoor hue
 He has never looked back since then
 bollywood ke shahenshaah, bollywood ke mahanayake, sadi ke mahanayake jaise upnaam unke saath judate gaye
 After completing 50 years in cinema, he will be awarded the Dadasaheb Phalke Award, the highest honor in the cinema world
 is khabar ke failte hi big bi ko badhaaiyaan milani shuru ho gai hai
 Information and Broadcasting Minister Prakash Javadekar shared this information on his official Twitter handle
 isi ke baad se unhen badhaaiyaan milane kaa silsilaa shuru ho gaya he
 They are also getting congratulations from Bollywood
 actor anil kapur, film diarector karan johar samet kai saare kalakaaron ne unhen shubhakamanaayen di hai

 pakistan ke pradhanmantri navaj sharif ne aaj kaha ki purv raashtrapati parvej musharraf ke khilaaf do baar desh ke samvidhan kaa ulanghan karne ke maamle main ghor rashtradroh ke mukadmaa chalaaya jayega
 If convicted, Musharraf could be sentenced to death or life imprisonment
 pradhanmantri ne jin do maamalon kaa zikr kiya he, unamem se pehla 1999 kaa takhtapalat or doosraa saal 2007 main apatkaal lagaakar nyaayadhishon ko barkhaast karne kaa he
 Sharif made the announcement in the National Assembly, the lower house of parliament, three weeks after his return to power
 sharif ne sansad ko bataaya ki musharraf kii ore se uthaae gaye kadam ‘ghor rashtradroh’ ke daayre main aate hai
 He said that Musharraf should face trial in the Supreme Court for his steps
 saal 2007 main apatkaal lagane ke musharraf ke faisle kaa hawala dete hue sharif ne kaha, sangheey sarkaar kaa yah thos vichaar he ki teen november, 2007 ko samvidhan ko darkinar karne kaa uthaaya gaya kadam pakistan ke samvidhan ke anuchhed 6 ke tahat ghor rajdroh ke tahat aata he
 PML-N leader Sharif said, the Prime Minister takes an oath to defend the Constitution
 is shapath main nihit he ki sarkaar anuchhed 6 ke tahat doshiyon ko nyaay ke jad main laaegi
 Sharif said that his government would deliberate to take all political parties into confidence in the context of prosecuting Musharraf
 sansad main sharif ke bayaan ke tatkaal baad atarni general munir malik ne sarkaar kii sthiti ke bare main supreme court kii us peeth ko suchit kiya, jo musharraf ke khilaaf ghor rashtradroh kaa maamla chalaane kii maang sambandhi yachika par sunwaayee kar rahi he
 The Attorney General says that the process of prosecuting Musharraf has begun, although the government needs 30 days for its future action
 udhar, pakistan kii sabase badi adaalat ne etorni general ko bhavishya ke kadam ke bare main faisle ke mahaj teen din kaa samay diya tathaa unhen aadesh diya ki sarkaar guuruuvaar tak apana jawaab daakhil kare
 Experts say the government may have to face pressure from the military, as it would not like to see one of its former generals being publicly humiliated
 tippaniyan According to Pakistan's constitution, only the government can decide the case in case of treason
 sharif ne kaha, musharraf ne do baar samvidhan kaa ulanghan kiya
 In 1999, he overthrew the elected government
 phir unhone nyaayadhishon ko bakhrast kar unhen najarband kar diya
 If convicted, Musharraf could be sentenced to death or life imprisonment
 pradhanmantri ne jin do maamalon kaa zikr kiya he, unamem se pehla 1999 kaa takhtapalat or doosraa saal 2007 main apatkaal lagaakar nyaayadhishon ko barkhaast karne kaa he

 sharif ne kaha, musharraf ne do baar samvidhan kaa ulanghan kiya
 In 1999, he overthrew the elected government
 phir unhone nyaayadhishon ko bakhrast kar unhen najarband kar diya
 Sharif told Parliament that the steps taken by Musharraf came under the purview of 'gross treason'
 unhone kaha ki musharraf ko unke kadamon ke liye supreme court main sunwaayee kaa saamana karnaa chahie
 Referring to Musharraf's decision to impose emergency in 2007, Sharif said, "it is a firm view of the federal government that on November 3, 2007, the steps taken to circumvent the constitution under gross treason under Article 6 of the Constitution of Pakistan" Comes
 piemail-en ke netaa sharif ne kaha, pradhanmantri samvidhan kii hifaazat karne kii shapath letaa he
 This oath implied that the government would bring the culprits to justice under Article 6
 sharif ne kaha ki unki sarkaar musharraf ke khilaaf mukadmaa chalaane ke sandarbh main sabhi raajnneetik dalon ko vishwaas main lene ke liye vichaar-vimarsh karegi
 Immediately after Sharif's statement in Parliament, Attorney General Munir Malik informed the bench of the Supreme Court about the government's position, which is hearing a petition seeking a case of gross treason against Musharraf
 atarni general kaa kahana he ki musharraf ke khilaaf mukadmaa chalaane kii prakriya aarambh ho chuki he, haalanki sarkaar ko apane bhavishya ke kadam ke liye 30 dinon ke samay kii jarurat he
 On the other hand, Pakistan's largest court gave the Attorney General just three days to decide the future course of action and ordered them to file their reply by Thursday
 jaankaron kaa kahana he ki sarkaar ko sena kii taraf se dabaav kaa saamana karnaa pad saktaa he, kyonki vah apane ek purv general ko saarvajanik rup se apamaanit hote nahin dekhnaa chaahegi
 The comments pakistan ke samvidhan ke anusaar, rashtradroh ke maamle main mukademe kaa faisla sirf sarkaar kar sakati he 
 Musharraf violated the Constitution twice, Sharif said
 1999 main unhone nirvaachit sarkaar kaa takhtapalat kiya
 He then dismissed the judges and placed them under house arrest

 The stock market investors' eyes will be mainly focused on the monetary policy review announcement of the Reserve Bank of India (RBI) in the coming week
 rigerv bank kii niti samiksha ghoshnaa mangalvaar (5 july) ko hogi

" jalaalekh surveykshan main hamaara sahyog vyapak hua he or bad rahaa he
